<p class="font_8" style="line-height:1.5em; text-align:center;"><span class="wixGuard"></span></p>

<p class="font_8" style="line-height:1.5em; text-align:center;">If you have recently come into contact with somebody who has been diagnosed with Covid-19 and have subsequently developed a suspicious&nbsp;illness yourself, use a comment in the forum below to log your earliest&nbsp;symptoms.&nbsp; Try to avoid&nbsp;generalised language e.g. &quot;Cold symptoms&quot;&nbsp;- instead try and be specific i.e. &quot;one cough every 15 minutes&quot;.</p>

<p class="font_8" style="line-height:1.5em; text-align:center;">Also try to explain to what extent you were able to function&nbsp;- were you able to sit upright, watch TV, leave bed, hold a conversation, could you make your own food...&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

<p class="font_8" style="line-height:1.5em; text-align:center;"><span class="wixGuard"></span></p></div><div data-packed="false" style="top:;bottom:;left:;right:;width:406px;height:auto;position:;min-height:152px;pointer-events:none" data-min-height="152" class="txtNew" id="comp-k7uheu17"><p class="font_8" style="font-size:20px; line-height:1.5em; text-align:center;"><span style="font-weight:bold;"><span style="font-size:20px;">Rate your illness on a scale of 0-10</span></span></p>

<p class="font_8" style="font-size:20px; line-height:1.5em; text-align:center;"><span style="font-weight:bold;"><span style="font-size:20px;">State your age-bracket</span></span></p>

<p class="font_8" style="font-size:20px; line-height:1.5em; text-align:center;"><span style="font-weight:bold;"><span style="font-size:20px;">Relevant pre-existing conditions</span></span></p>

<p class="font_8" style="font-size:20px; line-height:1.5em; text-align:center;"><span style="font-weight:bold;"><span style="font-size:20px;">List of symptoms</span></span></p></div><div data-border-width="1px" style="transform-origin:center 0.5px;top:;bottom:;left:;right:;width:800px;height:5px;position:" class="style-k7tmfxgo1" id="comp-k7tmfxgt"></div><div data-packed="false" style="top:;bottom:;left:;right:;width:591px;height:auto;position:;min-height:105px;pointer-events:none" data-min-height="105" class="txtNew" id="comp-k7ui7k9o"><p class="font_8">Use the subject line as follows:</p>

<p class="font_8"><span class="wixGuard"></span></p>
